<h1 _ngcontent-fnn-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.i18n (国际化-I18n)"> @ohos.i18n (国际化-I18n) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供系统相关的以及增强的<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-l10n" target="_blank">国际化</a>能力，包括区域管理、电话号码处理、日历等，相关接口为<a href="https://dev.ecma-international.org/publications-and-standards/standards/ecma-402/" target="_blank">ECMA 402</a>标准中未定义的补充接口。<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-intl">Intl模块</a>提供了ECMA 402标准定义的基础国际化接口，与本模块共同使用可提供完整地国际化能力。接口中使用的名词定义如下：</p>    <ul>     <li>模式字符串：由<a href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-dates.html#Date_Field_Symbol_Table" target="_blank">Unicode日期字段符号</a>和单引号包裹的自定义文本自由组合而成的字符串。</li>     <li>框架字符串：由<a href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-dates.html#Date_Field_Symbol_Table" target="_blank">Unicode日期字段符号</a>自由组合而成的字符串，不支持自定义文本。</li>    </ul>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>本模块首批接口从API version 7开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>本模块接口依据<a href="https://cldr.unicode.org" target="_blank">CLDR</a> 国际化数据库进行处理，随着CLDR演进，本模块接口处理结果可能发生变化。其中，API version 12对应<a href="https://cldr.unicode.org/index/downloads/cldr-42" target="_blank">CLDR 42</a>，具体数据变化请参考官方链接。</p></li>       <li>        <p>从API version 11开始，本模块部分接口支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;">     <h2 id="system9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">System<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="system9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>提供系统属性相关的能力，包括语言地区名称翻译、支持的语言地区列表获取和系统语言地区获取等。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1601px;">     <h3 id="getdisplaycountry9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">getDisplayCountry<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getdisplaycountry9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getDisplayCountry(country: string, locale: string, sentenceCase?: boolean): string</p>     <p>获取国家地区名称在指定语言下的翻译。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">country</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">国家地区，要求是<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">合法的国家地区码</a>。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">表示区域ID的字符串</a>，由语言、脚本、国家地区组成。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sentenceCase</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">true表示按照首字母大写的格式显示文本，false表示按照区域默认的大小写格式显示文本。默认值：true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">国家地区名称在指定语言下的翻译。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-i18n">ohos.i18n错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1.Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2.Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">890001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid parameter. Possible causes: Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>890001的报错信息请以接口的实际报错为准。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BusinessError</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li><li>

</div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 770px;">     <h3 id="getsystemlanguages9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getSystemLanguages<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getsystemlanguages9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span <p>获取系统支持的语言列表。</p>     <p>从API version 11开始，该类型支持在ArkTS卡片中使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Array&lt;string&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">系统支持的语言列表。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1548px;">     <h3 id="issuggested9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">isSuggested<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="issuggested9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static isSuggested(language: string, region?: string): boolean</p>     <p>判断语言是否是地区的推荐语言。用于根据地区推荐语言或根据语言推荐地区。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">language</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">合法的语言ID</a>，例如zh。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">region</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">合法的国家地区码</a>，例如CN。</p>          <p>默认值：SIM卡国家地区。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">true表示语言是地区的推荐语言，false表示语言不是地区的推荐语言。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a Possible causes: Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>890001的报错信息请以接口的实际报错为准。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BusinessError</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li><li>

id="setapppreferredlanguage11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setAppPreferredLanguage<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setapppreferredlanguage11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static setAppPreferredLanguage(language: string): void</p>     <p>设置应用偏好语言。设置后，应用将优先加载应用偏好语言对应的资源。设置偏好语言为'default'后，应用语言将跟随系统语言，应用冷启动生效。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">language</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">合法的语言ID</a>或'default'。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-i18n">ohos.i18n错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1.Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2.Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">890001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid parameter. Possible causes: Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BusinessError</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li><li>
</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {</li><li>  i18n.<span class="hljs-property">System</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">setAppPreferredLanguage</span>(<span id="getsimplifiedlanguage15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getSimplifiedLanguage<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getSimplifiedLanguage(language?: string): string</p>     <p>获取语言的简化表示。例如：'en-Latn-US'的简化表示为'en'，'en-Latn-GB'的简化表示为'en-GB'。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 15开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">language</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">合法的语言ID</a>。默认值：系统语言。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>不传入language时，会根据系统语言和地区判断是否存在系统支持的方言，若存在则返回方言的简化表示；若不存在，则返回系统语言的简化表示。</p>          <p>传入language时，返回language的简化表示。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a <p>判断语言是否为镜像语言。在镜像语言下，UI界面需要<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-ui-design#界面镜像" target="_blank">镜像显示</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;">     <h2 id="entityrecognizer11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EntityRecognizer<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="entityrecognizer11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>提供实体识别相关的能力，可以获取文本中实体的类型和起止位置。当前支持识别的实体包括电话号码和时间日期。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1200px;">     <h3 id="constructor11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">constructor<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="constructor11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>constructor(locale?: string)</p>     <p>创建实体识别对象。该对象根据区域规则识别文本中的实体。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.30.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">表示区域ID的字符串</a>，由语言、脚本、国家地区组成，例如zh-Hans-CN。</p>          <p>默认值：系统当前区域ID。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">isWeekend<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="isweekend8" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>isWeekend(date?: Date): boolean</p>     <p>判断指定的日期在日历对象中是否为周末。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">date</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Date</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>时间、日期。说明：月份从0开始计数，例如0表示一月。</p>          <p>默认值：日历对象的当前日期。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.45.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">true表示指定的日期是周末，false表示指定的日期不是周末。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> id="next8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">next<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>next(index?: number): number</p>     <p>将换行迭代器向后移动index个可换行点。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">index</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>换行迭代器将要移动的可换行点数，取值为整数。</p>          <p>正数表示向后移动index个可换行点，负数表示向前移动index个可换行点。</p>          <p>默认值：1。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>移动index个可换行点后，当前换行迭代器在文本中的位置。</p>          <p>若移动index个可换行点后超出了所处理的文本的长度范围，返回-1。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table <p>移动到前一个可换行点后，当前换行迭代器在文本中的位置。</p>          <p>若移动后超出了所处理的文本的长度范围，返回-1。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1017px;">     <h3 id="following8" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">following<sup>8+</sup><i class="anchor-icon 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">将换行迭代器移动到文本指定位置的后面一个可换行点。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">getMilliseconds<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;">     <h2 id="i18nutil9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">I18NUtil<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="i18nutil9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>国际化工具类，提供单位转换、获取日期顺序、获取时段名称、区域匹配和路径本地化等能力。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1229px;">     <h3 id="unitconvert9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">unitConvert<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="unitconvert9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static unitConvert(fromUnit: UnitInfo, toUnit: UnitInfo, value: number, locale: string, style?: string): string</p>     <p>将fromUnit的单位转换为toUnit的单位，并根据区域与风格进行格式化。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">fromUnit</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#unitinfo8">UnitInfo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要转换的单位。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">toUnit</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#unitinfo8">UnitInfo</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">转换成的目标单位。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">value</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">需要转换的单位的数量值。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">表示区域ID的字符串</a>，由语言、脚本、国家地区组成，如：zh-Hans-CN。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">style</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>格式化使用的风格，取值包括：'long', 'short', 'narrow'。默认值：short。</p>          <p>不同取值显示效果请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-numbers-weights-measures" target="_blank">数字与度量衡国际化</a>。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.105.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">转换单位后的度量衡格式化结果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> liters'</span></li></ol></pre></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 921px;">     <h3 id="getdateorder9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getDateOrder<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getdateorder9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getDateOrder(locale: string): string</p>     <p>获取某区域日期中年、月、日的排列顺序。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.106.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.106.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left"     <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">该区域年、月、日的排列顺序。“y”表示年，“L”表示月，“d”表示日。</td>        </tr> class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1432px;">     <h3 id="gettimeperiodname11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getTimePeriodName<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon id="getbestmatchlocale12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getBestMatchLocale<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getBestMatchLocale(locale: string, localeList: string[]): string</p>     <p>在指定区域列表中获取与某个区域最佳匹配的区域。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1387px;">     <h3 id="getthreeletterlanguage12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getThreeLetterLanguage<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getthreeletterlanguage12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getThreeLetterLanguage(locale: string): string</p>     <p>将语言代码由二字母转换为三字母。二字母和三字母语言代码的规格参考<a href="https://www.iso.org/iso-639-language-code" target="_blank">ISO 639</a>。</p>     <p>例如，中文的二字母语言代码是zh，对应的三字母语言代码是zho。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">待转换的语言二字母代码，如：zh。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回待转换语言二字母代码对应的三字母代码。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-i18n">ohos.i18n错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.109.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1.Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2.Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">890001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid parameter. Possible causes: Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BusinessError</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li><li>

class="hljs-property">I18NUtil</span>.<span class="hljs-title function_">getThreeLetterLanguage</span>(<span class="hljs-string">'zh'</span>) <span class="hljs-comment">// language = 'zho'</span></li><li>} <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (error) {</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> <span class="hljs-attr">err</span>: <span class="hljs-title id="getthreeletterregion12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getThreeLetterRegion<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="getthreeletterregion12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static getThreeLetterRegion(locale: string): string</p>     <p>将地区代码由二字母转换为三字母。二字母和三字母地区代码的规格参考<a href="https://www.iso.org/iso-3166-country-codes.html" target="_blank">ISO 3166</a></p>     <p>例如，中国的二字母地区代码是CN, 三字母是CHN。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">待转换的地区二字母代码，如：CN。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回待转换地区二字母代码对应的三字母代码。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-i18n">ohos.i18n错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.13.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.110.13.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1.Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2.Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">890001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Invalid parameter. Possible causes: Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-title class_">BusinessError</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.BasicServicesKit'</span>;</li><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { i18n } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.LocalizationKit'</span>;</li><li>

id="getunicodewrappedfilepath20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">getUnicodeWrappedFilePath<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" <p>对文件路径进行本地化处理。</p>     <p>例如，将/data/out/tmp本地化处理后生成tmp/out/data/。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>     <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">path</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td target="_blank">Intl.Locale</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">区域对象，默认值：系统区域对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1457px;">     <h2 id="i18ngetsimpledatetimeformatbypattern20" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">i18n.getSimpleDateTimeFormatByPattern<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="i18ngetsimpledatetimeformatbypattern20" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getSimpleDateTimeFormatByPattern(pattern: string, locale?: Intl.Locale): SimpleDateTimeFormat</p>     <p>通过模式字符串获取SimpleDateTimeFormat对象。与<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#i18ngetsimpledatetimeformatbyskeleton20">getSimpleDateTimeFormatBySkeleton</a>接口获取的对象在格式化后显示差异请参考<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#format18">SimpleDateTimeFormat.format</a>的示例。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 20开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">pattern</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">合法的模式字符串，支持<a href="https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr35/tr35-dates.html#Date_Field_Symbol_Table" target="_blank">日期字段符号表</a>中Field Patterns值的自由组合。同时，pattern支持传入自定义文本，文本内容以''标识。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Intl/Locale" target="_blank">Intl.Locale</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">区域对象。默认值：系统区域对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.123.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#simpledatetimeformat18">SimpleDateTimeFormat</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">SimpleDateTimeFormat对象。</td>        </tr> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">format<sup>18+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1067px;">     <h2 id="i18ngetdisplaycountrydeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">i18n.getDisplayCountry<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="i18ngetdisplaycountrydeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getDisplayCountry(country: string, locale: string, sentenceCase?: boolean): string</p>     <p>从API version 7开始支持，从API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#getdisplaycountry9">System.getDisplayCountry</a>替代。</p>     <p>获取指定国家的本地化名称。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">country</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">指定国家。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">locale</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/i18n-locale-culture#实现原理" target="_blank">表示区域ID的字符串</a>，由语言、脚本、国家地区组成。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">sentenceCase</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">boolean</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">true表示按照首字母大写的格式显示文本，false表示按照区域默认的大小写格式显示文本。默认值：true。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.138.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">指定国家的本地化显示文本。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-fnn-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="gettypedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getType(ch: string): string</p>     <p>从API version 8开始支持，从API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-i18n#gettype9">getType</a>替代。</p>     <p>获取输入的字符的一般类别值。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Global.I18n</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.160.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.160.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.160.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.160.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ch</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">输入的字符。如果输入的是字符串，则只判断首字符的类别。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table
